direction. End points are plotted relative to the planned target point, indicated as each zero point. Axes
correspond to the XY plane, tangent to the planned target point (as seen in Figs. 1A and 3B), onto which the
relative position of the achieved end points is projected, indicating the deviation in each axis direction in
millimeters.
